<script>
$("#pagination-hook a").each(function(index) { 
	var text = $(this).attr("href")
	var index = text.lastIndexOf("=")
	var pageNumber = text.substring(index + 1)
	$(this).attr("onclick", "return setPage(" + pageNumber + ", this)"); $(this).attr("oncontextmenu", "setPage(" + pageNumber + ", this)");
})
</script>
